#cheat Cops Shoot Away From Flamethrower
//ID: 5563
//Score: 58
//Author: theY4Kman
//Category: Pedestrians
//Description: When you have a wanted level, and you have cops shooting and/or bashing you with the night stick, taking out the flamethrower and shooting the opposite makes the cops with guns spaz out and shoot the way the flamethrower isn't going.
//Image: none
//Time: 11/03/2006 15:18:16
//Working: Yes
sethex(08b312D4, 2B);
sethex(08b312D5, 14);
sethex(08b312D6, 2D);
sethex(08b312D7, 04);
